[30;1m7 | [0m[35mFlask-Caching is an extension to `Flask`_ that adds caching support for[0m
[30;1m8 | [0m[35mvarious backends to any Flask application. By running on top of `cachelib`_[0m
[30;1m9 | [0m[35mit supports all of `werkzeug`_'s original caching backends through a uniformed[0m
[30;1m10 | [0m[35mAPI. It is also possible to develop your own caching backend by subclassing[0m
[30;1m11 | [0m[35m:class:`flask_caching.backends.base.BaseCache` class.[0m
